## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    Idle --> Fetching : fetchSubscription / fetchUserSubscriptions
    Fetching --> Success : data received
    Fetching --> Error : network/error
    Success --> Idle
    Error --> Idle
    Idle --> Updating : subscribe/update/unsubscribe/delete
    Updating --> UpdateSuccess
    Updating --> UpdateError
    UpdateSuccess --> Idle
    UpdateError --> Idle
```
